href=\"https://github.com/kamilsss655/uv-k5-firmware-custom/wiki/44-%E2%80%90-Encryption#details\"\u003eEncryption\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFixed AM AGC so \u003cstrong\u003eAM demodulation is crystal clear\u003c/strong\u003e, no audible clicks, no need for \u003ccode\u003eAM_FIX\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eRxOff\u003c/code\u003e menu setting offsets the receive frequency by any specified amount in the range of \u003ccode\u003e0-150Mhz\u003c/code\u003e for use with upconverters. Allows to fine tune frequency (in \u003ccode\u003e1kHz\u003c/code\u003e steps) as opposed to other implementations that use hardcoded offsets. (\u003cstrong\u003eIMPORTANT: Make sure you set this value to 0 if not using an upconverter, when used for the first time. Otherwise it might load some random offset from EEPROM.\u003c/strong\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eENABLE_SPECTRUM_COPY_VFO\u003c/code\u003e allowing to exit the spectrum and fine tuning screen with PTT button and copy current peak frequency, modulation, step, bandwidth to VFO. Also entering spectrum will carry these settings from VFO (full integration). Now to enter fine tuning screen in spectrum press MENU button. This allows you to save and respond to the frequencies found much faster.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eENABLE_SPECTRUM_SHOW_CHANNEL_NAME\u003c/code\u003e shows channel number and channel name of the peak frequency in spectrum\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eENABLE_ADJUSTABLE_RX_GAIN_SETTINGS\u003c/code\u003e keeps the rx gain settings set in spectrum mode after exit (otherwise these are always overwritten to default value), this makes much more sense considering that we have a radio with user adjustable gain so why not use it to adjust to current radio conditions, maximum gain allows to greatly increase reception in scan memory channels mode (in this configuration default gain settings are only set at boot and when exiting AM modulation mode to set it to sane value after am fix)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eVOXSen\u003c/code\u003e fixed and improved VOX sensitivity setting from menu. Added \u003ccode\u003eVoxDel\u003c/code\u003e - VOX delay setting allowing to set value to \u003ccode\u003e0\u003c/code\u003e for no VOX delay which might be useful for packet radio enthusiasts (APRS etc.).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eSqTone\u003c/code\u003e configurable squelch tail tones and 180* phase shift tail when in CTCSS mode\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-alert markdown-alert-note\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cp class=\"markdown-alert-title\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-info mr-2\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"M0 8a8 8 0 1 1 16 0A8 8 0 0 1 0 8Zm8-6.5a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 0 13 6.5 6.5 0 0 0 0-13ZM6.5 7.75A.75.75 0 0 1 7.25 performance\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-radio-performance\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Radio performance\" href=\"#radio-performance\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePlease note that the Quansheng UV-Kx radios are not professional quality transceivers, their\nperformance is strictly limited. The RX front end has no track-tuned band pass filtering\nat all, and so are wide band/wide open to any and all signals over a large frequency range.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUsing the radio in high intensity RF environments will most likely make reception anything but\neasy (AM mode will suffer far more than FM ever will), the receiver simply doesn't have a\ngreat dynamic range, which results in distorted AM audio with stronger RX'ed signals.\nThere is nothing more anyone can do in firmware/software to improve that, once the RX gain\nadjustment I do (AM fix) reaches the hardwares limit, your AM RX audio will be all but\nnon-existent (just like Quansheng's firmware).\nOn the other hand, FM RX audio will/should be fine.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBut, they are nice toys for the price, fun to play with.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eUser customization\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-user-customization\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: User customization\" href=\"#user-customization\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eYou can customize the firmware by enabling/disabling various compile options, this allows\nus to remove certain firmware features in order to make room in the flash for others.\nYou'll find the options at the top of \"Makefile\" ('0' = disable, '1' = enable) ..\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"ENABLE_CLANG                       := 0     **experimental, builds with clang instead of gcc (LTO will be disabled if you enable this)\nENABLE_SWD                         := 0       only needed if using CPU's SWD port (debugging/programming)\nENABLE_OVERLAY                     := 0       cpu FLASH stuff, not needed\nENABLE_LTO                         := 1     **experimental, reduces size of compiled firmware but might break EEPROM reads (OVERLAY will be disabled if you enable this)\n\nENABLE_UART                        := 1       without this you can't configure radio via PC !\nENABLE_AIRCOPY                     := 0       easier to just enter frequency with butts\nENABLE_FMRADIO                     := 1       WBFM VHF broadcast band receiver\nENABLE_NOAA                        := 0       everything NOAA (only of any use in the USA)\nENABLE_VOICE                       := 0       want to hear voices ?\nENABLE_VOX                         := 1\nENABLE_ALARM                       := 0       TX alarms\nENABLE_TX1750                      := 0       side key 1750Hz TX tone (older style repeater access)\nENABLE_PWRON_PASSWORD              := 0       power-on password stuff\nENABLE_DTMF_CALLING                := 0       DTMF calling fuctionality, sending calls, receiving calls, group calls, contacts list etc.\n\nENABLE_BIG_FREQ                    := 1       big font frequencies (like original QS firmware)\nENABLE_SMALL_BOLD                  := 1       bold channel name/no. (when name + freq channel display mode)\nENABLE_KEEP_MEM_NAME               := 1       maintain channel name when (re)saving memory channel\nENABLE_WIDE_RX                     := 1       full 18MHz to 1300MHz RX (though front-end/PA not designed for full range)\nENABLE_TX_WHEN_AM                  := 0       allow TX (always FM) when RX is set to AM\nENABLE_F_CAL_MENU                  := 0       enable the radios hidden frequency calibration menu\nENABLE_SHOW_CHARGE_LEVEL           := 0       show the charge level when the radio is on charge\nENABLE_REVERSE_BAT_SYMBOL          := 0       mirror the battery symbol on the status bar (+ pole on the right)\nENABLE_NO_CODE_SCAN_TIMEOUT        := 1       disable 32-sec CTCSS/DCS scan timeout (press exit butt instead of time-out to end scan)\nENABLE_SQUELCH_MORE_SENSITIVE      := 0       make squelch levels a little bit more sensitive - this has been reported to cause radio freeze in presence of strong signals\nENABLE_FASTER_CHANNEL_SCAN         := 1       increases the channel scan speed, but the squelch is also made more twitchy\nENABLE_RSSI_BAR                    := 1       enable a dBm/Sn RSSI bar graph level in place of the little antenna symbols\nENABLE_AUDIO_BAR                   := 1       experimental, display an audio bar level when TX'ing\nENABLE_COPY_CHAN_TO_VFO            := 1       copy current channel into the other VFO. Long press `1 BAND` when in channel mode\nENABLE_SPECTRUM                    := 1       fagci spectrum analyzer, activated with `F` + `5 NOAA`\nENABLE_REDUCE_LOW_POWER            := 1       makes low power settings even lower (L=0.45W M=3W H=4.7W (f=147Mhz))\nENABLE_BYP_RAW_DEMODULATORS        := 0       additional BYP (bypass?) and RAW demodulation options, proved not to be very useful, but it is there if you want to experiment\nENABLE_BLMIN_TMP_OFF               := 0       additional function for configurable buttons that toggles `BLMin` on and off wihout saving it to the EEPROM\nENABLE_SCAN_RANGES                 := 1       scan range mode for frequency scanning, see wiki for instructions (radio operation -\u0026gt; frequency scanning)\nENABLE_SPECTRUM_COPY_VFO           := 1       pressing MENU in spectrum mode will exit and copy current peak frequency, bw, step, modulation to current VFO, also entering spectrum will carry these settings from VFO (full integration)\nENABLE_SPECTRUM_SHOW_CHANNEL_NAME  := 1       shows channel number and channel name of the peak frequency in spectrum\nENABLE_ADJUSTABLE_RX_GAIN_SETTINGS := 1       keeps the rx gain settings set in spectrum mode after exit (otherwise these are always overwritten to default value), this makes much more sense considering that we have a radio with user adjustable gain so why not use it to adjust to current radio conditions, maximum gain allows to greatly increase reception in scan memory channels mode (in this configuration default gain settings are only set at boot and when exiting AM modulation mode to set it to sane value after am fix)\nENABLE_SPECTRUM_CHANNEL_SCAN       := 1       this enables spectrum channel scan mode (enter by going into memory mode and press F+5, this allows SUPER fast channel scanning (4.5x faster than regular scanning), regular scan of 200 memory channels takes roughly 18 seconds, spectrum memory scan takes roughly 4 seconds, if you have less channels stored i.e 50 - the spectrum memory scan will take only **1 second**\nENABLE_MESSENGER                   := 1       enable messenger\nENABLE_MESSENGER_FSK_MUTE          := 1       mutes speaker once it detects fsk sync word (might cause unintentional mutes during ctcss rx)\nENABLE_MESSENGER_NOTIFICATION      := 1       enable messenger delivery notification\nENABLE_MESSENGER_UART              := 0       enable sending messages via serial with SMS:content command (unreliable)\nENABLE_ENCRYPTION                  := 1       enable ChaCha20 256 bit encryption for messenger\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003eENABLE_CLANG                       := 0     **experimental, builds with clang instead of gcc (LTO will be disabled if you enable this)\nENABLE_SWD                         := 0       only needed if using CPU's SWD port (debugging/programming)\nENABLE_OVERLAY                     := 0       cpu FLASH stuff, not needed\nENABLE_LTO                         := 1     **experimental, reduces size of compiled firmware but might break EEPROM reads (OVERLAY will be disabled if you enable this)\n\nENABLE_UART                        := 1       without this you can't configure radio via PC !\nENABLE_AIRCOPY                     := 0       easier to just enter frequency with butts\nENABLE_FMRADIO                     := 1       WBFM VHF broadcast band receiver\nENABLE_NOAA                        := 0       everything NOAA (only of any use in the USA)\nENABLE_VOICE                       := 0       want to hear voices ?\nENABLE_VOX                         := 1\nENABLE_ALARM                       := 0       TX alarms\nENABLE_TX1750                      := 0       side key 1750Hz TX tone (older style repeater access)\nENABLE_PWRON_PASSWORD              := 0       power-on password stuff\nENABLE_DTMF_CALLING                := 0       DTMF calling fuctionality, sending calls, receiving calls, group calls, contacts list etc.\n\nENABLE_BIG_FREQ                    := 1       big font frequencies (like original QS firmware)\nENABLE_SMALL_BOLD                  := 1       bold channel name/no. (when name + freq channel display mode)\nENABLE_KEEP_MEM_NAME               := 1       maintain channel name when (re)saving memory channel\nENABLE_WIDE_RX                     := 1       full 18MHz to 1300MHz RX (though front-end/PA not designed for full range)\nENABLE_TX_WHEN_AM                  := 0       allow TX (always FM) when RX is set to AM\nENABLE_F_CAL_MENU                  := 0       enable the radios hidden frequency calibration menu\nENABLE_SHOW_CHARGE_LEVEL           := 0       show the charge level when the radio is on charge\nENABLE_REVERSE_BAT_SYMBOL          := 0       mirror the battery symbol on the status bar (+ pole on the right)\nENABLE_NO_CODE_SCAN_TIMEOUT        := 1       disable 32-sec CTCSS/DCS scan timeout (press exit butt instead of time-out to end scan)\nENABLE_SQUELCH_MORE_SENSITIVE      := 0       make squelch levels a little bit more sensitive - this has been reported to cause radio freeze in presence of strong signals\nENABLE_FASTER_CHANNEL_SCAN         := 1       increases the channel scan speed, but the squelch is also made more twitchy\nENABLE_RSSI_BAR                    := 1       enable a dBm/Sn RSSI bar graph level in place of the little antenna symbols\nENABLE_AUDIO_BAR                   := 1       experimental, display an audio bar level when TX'ing\nENABLE_COPY_CHAN_TO_VFO            := 1       copy current channel into the other VFO. Long press `1 BAND` when in channel mode\nENABLE_SPECTRUM                    := 1       fagci spectrum analyzer, activated with `F` + `5 NOAA`\nENABLE_REDUCE_LOW_POWER            := 1       makes low power settings even lower (L=0.45W M=3W H=4.7W (f=147Mhz))\nENABLE_BYP_RAW_DEMODULATORS        := 0       additional BYP (bypass?) and RAW demodulation options, proved not to be very useful, but it is there if you want to experiment\nENABLE_BLMIN_TMP_OFF               := 0       additional function for configurable buttons that toggles `BLMin` on and off wihout saving it to the EEPROM\nENABLE_SCAN_RANGES                 := 1       scan range mode for frequency scanning, see wiki for instructions (radio operation -\u0026gt; frequency scanning)\nENABLE_SPECTRUM_COPY_VFO           := 1       pressing MENU in spectrum mode will exit and copy current peak frequency, bw, step, modulation to current VFO, also entering spectrum will carry these settings from VFO (full integration)\nENABLE_SPECTRUM_SHOW_CHANNEL_NAME  := 1       shows channel number and channel name of the peak frequency in spectrum\nENABLE_ADJUSTABLE_RX_GAIN_SETTINGS := 1       keeps the rx gain settings set in spectrum mode after exit (otherwise these are always overwritten to default value), this makes much more sense considering that we have a radio with user adjustable gain so why not use it to adjust to current radio conditions, maximum gain allows to greatly increase reception in scan memory channels mode (in this configuration default gain settings are only set at boot and when exiting AM modulation mode to set it to sane value after am fix)\nENABLE_SPECTRUM_CHANNEL_SCAN       := 1       this enables spectrum channel scan mode (enter by going into memory mode and press F+5, this allows SUPER fast channel scanning (4.5x faster than regular scanning), regular scan of 200 memory channels takes roughly 18 seconds, spectrum memory scan takes roughly 4 seconds, if you have less channels stored i.e 50 - the spectrum memory scan will take only **1 second**\nENABLE_MESSENGER                   := 1       enable messenger\nENABLE_MESSENGER_FSK_MUTE          := 1       mutes speaker once it detects fsk sync word (might cause unintentional mutes during ctcss rx)\nENABLE_MESSENGER_NOTIFICATION      := 1       enable messenger delivery notification\nENABLE_MESSENGER_UART              := 0       enable sending messages via serial with SMS:content command (unreliable)\nENABLE_ENCRYPTION                  := 1       enable ChaCha20 256 bit encryption for messenger\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" current version on Ubuntu 22.04.03 LTS.\nOther versions may generate a flash file that is too big.\nYou can get an appropriate version from: \u003ca This method gives significantly smaller binaries, I've seen differences up to 1kb, so it can fit more functionalities this way. The challenge can be (or not) installing docker itself.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eTo compile:\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv
